If this circuit breaker overflows the :ref:`upstream_cx_overflow\n16:   <config_cluster_manager_cluster_stats>` counter for the cluster will increment. All connections,\n17:   whether active or draining, count against this limit. Even if this circuit breaker has overflowed,\n18:   Envoy will ensure that a host selected by cluster load balancing has at least one connection\n19:   allocated. This has the implication that the :ref:`upstream_cx_active\n20:   <config_cluster_manager_cluster_stats>` count for a cluster may be higher than the cluster maximum\n21:   connection circuit breaker, with an upper bound of\n22:   ``cluster maximum connections + (number of endpoints in a cluster) * (connection pools for the\n23:   cluster)``.
